<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">terwilen</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> shortening <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilen.html>wilen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:that.html>that</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:see.html>See</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>also</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijl.html>wijl</a></i>.

<li>whereas

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tevreden.html>tevreden</a> (1549)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tevreden.html>tevreden</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> univerbation <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vreden.html>vreden</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">zufrieden</i>.
</p>

***theatraal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:theatraal.html>theatraal</a> (25567)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">théâtral</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">theātrālis</i>.

***thee.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a> (1189)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowing <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms">teh</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Min" class="extiw" title="w:Southern Min"><a href = vnd.unilang:min.html>Min</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nan.html>Nan</a></a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="nan">茶</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="nan-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tê</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> "-h-" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> Faux-Greek <a href = vnd.unilang:spelling.html>spelling</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language"><a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">τσάι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tsái</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Kopje_thee.jpg/250px-Kopje_thee.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="188" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Kopje_thee.jpg/375px-Kopje_thee.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Kopje_thee.jpg/500px-Kopje_thee.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1152" data-file-height="864" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i><a href = vnd.unilang:gevuld.html>Gevuld</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a></b><a href = vnd.unilang:glas.html>glas</a></i><br />Filled <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tea.html>tea</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:glass.html>glass</a></div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>theeën</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>theetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">θέμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">théma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
